class=\"container\">\n\n    \t\n    <div class=\"container\" role=\"main\">\n        <div class=\"row column-content-wrapper\">\n\n            \n                <div id=\"content\" class=\"span9 article-container tc-gallery-style\">\n\n                    \n                        \n                                                                                    \n                                                                    <article id=\"page-13\" class=\"row-fluid post-13 page type-page status-publish hentry\">\n                                        \n                <div class=\"entry-content\">\n                    <div class=\"fpc-container fpc-marketing\">\n<div class=\"fpc-row-fluid fpc-widget-area rounded\">\n<div class=\"fpc-span4 fp-one\">\n<div class=\"fpc-widget-front\">\n<div class=\"thumb-wrapper\"><img class=\"attachment-medium tc-thumb-type-thumb wp-post-image h-centered tc-smart-loaded\" style=\"height: 250px; width: auto; left: -56px; top: -2px; display: inline;\" src=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/hadoop-icon-grid.png\" alt=\"wand\" width=\"270\" height=\"250\"></div>\n<h2 class=\"fp-title text-random-override\">Hadoop</h2>\n<p class=\"fp-excerpt fp-text-one text-random-override\">Opportunities don’t just happen You need to create it.</p>\n<p><a class=\"fpc-btn fpc-btn-primary fp-button none btn-random-override \" title=\"Hadoop\" href=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/hadoop-developer-course-contents/\" target=\"_blank\" data-color=\"none\">Read more »</a></p>\n</div>\n<p><!-- /.fpc-widget-front --></p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"fpc-span4 fp-two\">\n<div class=\"fpc-widget-front\">\n<div class=\"thumb-wrapper\"><img class=\"attachment-medium tc-thumb-type-thumb wp-post-image h-centered tc-smart-loaded\" style=\"height: 250px; width: auto; left: -56px; top: -2px; display: inline;\" src=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/scala-icon-grid.png\" alt=\"plus\" width=\"270\" height=\"250\"></div>\n<h2 class=\"fp-title text-random-override\">Scala</h2>\n<p class=\"fp-excerpt fp-text-two text-random-override\">Open the World with Scala Object Oriented language.</p>\n<p><a class=\"fpc-btn fpc-btn-primary fp-button none btn-random-override \" title=\"Scala\" href=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/spark-course-contents/\" target=\"_blank\" data-color=\"none\">Read more »</a></p>\n</div>\n<p><!-- /.fpc-widget-front --></p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"fpc-span4 fp-three\">\n<div class=\"fpc-widget-front\">\n<div class=\"thumb-wrapper\"><img class=\"attachment-medium tc-thumb-type-thumb wp-post-image h-centered tc-smart-loaded\" style=\"height: 250px; width: auto; left: -56px; top: -2px; display: inline;\" src=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/wp-content/uploads/2015/08/spark-icon-grid.png\" alt=\"html5\" width=\"270\" height=\"250\"></div>\n<h2 class=\"fp-title text-random-override\">Spark</h2>\n<p class=\"fp-excerpt fp-text-three text-random-override\">Full Insight of the Spark and Crystal details of its usage.</p>\n<p><a class=\"fpc-btn fpc-btn-primary fp-button none btn-random-override \" title=\"Spark\" href=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/spark-course-contents/\" target=\"_blank\" data-color=\"none\">Read more »</a></p>\n</div>\n<p><!-- /.fpc-widget-front --></p>\n</div>\n</div>\n<p><!--/fpc-row-1--></p>\n</div>\n<div class=\"clear clearfix\"></div>\n<h5 lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;\">What is Hadoop ?</span></h5>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Hadoop is an open source frame work used for storing &amp; processing large-scale data (huge data sets generally in GBs or TBs or PBs of size) which can be either structured or unstructured format. This vast amount of data is called Big data which usually can’t be processed/handled by legacy data storage mechanisms.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Hadoop is written in java by Apache Software Foundation. Hadoop can easily handle multi tera bytes of data reliably and in fault-tolerant manner.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Hadoop parallelizes the processing of the data on 1000s of computers or nodes in clusters. This frame work uses normal commodity hardware for storing distributed data across various nodes on the cluster.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">This Site provides detailed walk through of the Hadoop framework along with all the sub components under Hadoop Frame work.</p>\n<h6 lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;\"><strong>Hadoop Eco System Core Components:</strong></span></h6>\n<ul style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Hadoop Common</strong>&nbsp;:&nbsp;<strong>Common utilities supporting hadoop components</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">HDFS</strong> : <strong> Hadoop Distributed File System</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">YARN</strong> :&nbsp;<strong>Frame work for job scheduling and resource management.</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Map Reduce</strong>&nbsp;: <strong>&nbsp;Parallel Processing Mechanism for distributed data</strong></li>\n</ul>\n<h6 lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;\"><strong>The sub components are:</strong></span></h6>\n<ul style=\"text-align: justify;\">\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Hbase</strong> : <strong>&nbsp;Column Oriented Database for Processing Billions of Records</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Hive</strong> : &nbsp;<strong> Data Warehouse for Distributed File System HDFS</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Pig</strong>&nbsp;: &nbsp;<strong>High Level Programming Language for Distributed computations</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Sqoop</strong> : &nbsp;<strong>Data migration tool from/to RDBMSs to/from HDFS, HBase, Hive</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Flume</strong> : &nbsp;<strong>Data Collection mechanism for Log &amp; Event data</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Oozie</strong> : <strong>Work Flow Management Service.</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">ZooKeeper</strong> &nbsp;: &nbsp;<strong>Configuration Management &amp; Coordination Service.</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Avro</strong> &nbsp;: &nbsp;<strong>Serialization Framework</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Tez</strong>&nbsp;: &nbsp;<strong>Successor for Mapreduce Framework</strong></li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Hcatalog</strong> &nbsp;: <strong>Common Interface for Hive, Pig, HBase</strong>.</li>\n<li><strong class=\"components\">Azkaban</strong>: <strong>Workflow management tool.&nbsp;Alternative to Oozie.</strong></li>\n</ul>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Refer Corresponding Categories on this blog&nbsp;for further details on each sub component of Hadoop Eco System.</p>\n<p>&nbsp;</p>\n<h5 lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;\"><strong>Why Hadoop ? :</strong></span></h5>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Now a day</strong>&nbsp;the electronic data is getting increased rapidly day by day in terms of tera bytes (1000 GB = 1 TB) or peta bytes (1000 TB = 1 PB) all over world. This data is majorly stored on databases, distributed across the globe.&nbsp;<strong>The rate of data increase is getting accelerated</strong>. Some of the data might be structural and some might be unstructured data like flat data sets. Some of the examples of huge data generations sources are like social networking sites, blogs, databases and many other kinds of web sites. This data is being used by various organizations/industries for analyzing and foreseeing trends of business in near future based on the analysis of current data statistics.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>But extraction &amp; analysis of vast amount of structured data or unstructured data requires lot of computational power which is beyond the scope of legacy databases</strong>&nbsp;or processing techniques. This massive explosion of data over the years leads many organizations to replace the data servers with high processing servers which couldn’t solve the problem beyond a certain point of growth in data.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">That’s where the&nbsp;<strong>Hadoop evolution started based on scale-out approach</strong>&nbsp;for storing big data on large clusters of commodity hardware. Since Hadoop is designed to use commodity hardware through scale-out approach instead of using the larger servers in scale-up approach,&nbsp;<strong>data storage and maintenance became very cheap and cost effective when compared to other storage mechanisms</strong>.</p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">For processing this Big data, distributed across various clusters of commodity hardware,&nbsp;<strong>Map Reduce technique is introduced to parallelize the process of data extractions &amp; processing of structured/unstructured data from many nodes/hard drives in the clusters.</strong></p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Hadoop was created by Doug Cutting,</strong>&nbsp;who is the creator of Apache Lucene, a text search library.&nbsp;<strong>Hadoop was written in Java</strong>&nbsp;and has its origins from Apache Nutch, an open source web search engine. As Apache Software Foundation developed Hadoop, it is often called as&nbsp;<strong>Apache Hadoop</strong>&nbsp;and it&nbsp;<strong>is a Open Source frame work and available for free downloads from Apache Hadoop Distributions.</strong></p>\n<p lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\">Now, start reading from <span style=\"color: #0000ff;\"><a href=\"http://staging.hadooptutorial.info/category/hadoop/\" target=\"_blank\"><span style=\"color: #0000ff;\">Hadoop</span></a></span>&nbsp;blog to start learning hadoop from scratch.</p>\n<p><!--\n\n\n<div class=\"testimonial\">\n\n\n<h6 lang=\"en-US\" style=\"text-align: justify;\"><span style=\"text-decoration: underline; color: #0000ff;\"><strong>What Experts say ?</strong></span></h6>\n\n\n[testimonials_cycle show_thumbs='1' pager='1' easy_testimonial_title='1' itemprop=\"name\"]</div>\n\n\n--></p>\n<div class=\"sharedaddy sd-sharing-enabled\"><div class=\"robots-nocontent sd-block sd-social sd-social-official sd-sharing\"><h3 class=\"sd-title\">Share this:</h3><div class=\"sd-content\"><ul><li class=\"share-facebook\"><div class=\"fb-share-button fb_iframe_widget\" data-href=\"http://hadooptutorial.info/\" data-layout=\"button_count\" fb-xfbml-state=\"rendered\" fb-iframe-plugin-query=\"app_id=249643311490&amp;container_width=0&amp;href=http%3A%2F%2Fhadooptutorial.info%2F&amp;layout=button_count&amp;locale=en_US&amp;sdk=joey\"><span style=\"vertical-align: bottom;
